FNV PPLIGHTING LOW-LEVEL RENDER-STATE APPLY CONTRACT AUDIT

Questions:
1. What does E890C0 apply when called by E7DE90 with pass-mode table values?
2. What does E89410 validate or apply for E7EB00 pass-entry indexes?
3. Does E7EA00 reach texture, texture-stage, sampler, or only render-state calls?
4. Do any low-level apply helpers call E88A20, E88930, or E910A0 directly or indirectly?
5. Are tables 0x0126F680, 0x0126F0B0, and 0x0126F0B4 texture-stage maps or non-texture pass-state caches?
